## QR ONBOARDING RPCs (migration 248 — slice 1 routing layer)

Generic `invite_links` routing layer. Stable code → mutable destination;
the QR encodes only `/q/<code>`. Plan: `QR_ONBOARDING_SCOPE.md`; design:
DECISIONS.md "QR ONBOARDING ARCHITECTURE".

| RPC | JS wrapper | Grant | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| `resolve_invite_link(p_code)` | `resolveInviteLink(code)` | anon + authenticated | **Read-only** (STABLE, SECURITY DEFINER, search_path locked). Resolves a scanned code → `{ok, status, code, action, entity_type, entity_id, destination}`. `status ∈ ok\|inactive\|expired\|exhausted\|not_found`. `destination` is minimal per action (team→`{team_id,team_name}`; venue→`{venue_id,venue_name,logo_url,colours}`; fixture→`{fixture_id}`) — richer data comes from each action's own RPC. NULL destination (target entity gone) → status `not_found`. **Consumers (hard-rule #14)**: `apps/inorout` `InviteResolve.jsx` (`/q/<code>`); slice 3 venue landing; slice 6 check-in. |
| `redeem_invite_link(p_code)` | `redeemInviteLink(code)` | anon + authenticated | **Write** (VOLATILE, SECURITY DEFINER, search_path locked). Atomic `use_count++` under `FOR UPDATE`, re-checks active/expiry/max_uses in-txn (race-safe); refuses invalid without incrementing. INSERTs `audit_events` (`action='invite_link_redeemed'`, `actor_type='system'`, scope `team_id`=entity_id for team/venue; Hard Rule #9). Slice 1 handles team + venue; the **fixture branch raises `checkin_redeem_not_built`** until slice 6 adds it. Call AFTER the action succeeds (post-join), NOT on scan. EV-verified (resolve/redeem/status-paths/audit-trace/fixture-deferred, 6 assertions, leak 0); rpc-security-sweep PASS (secdef, search_path, 1 overload, anon+auth granted, PUBLIC revoked). **Consumers (hard-rule #14)**: slice 2 post-join hook (shipped); slice 3 venue-landing registration (shipped); slice 6 check-in. |
| `venue_ensure_invite_link(p_credential, p_entity_type, p_entity_id, p_action)` | `venueEnsureInviteLink(credential, entityType, entityId, action)` | anon + authenticated | **Write** (VOLATILE, SECURITY DEFINER, search_path locked) — mig 251, slice 4. The "code provider" the venue QR view + reception display read: get-or-creates the ONE canonical active `invite_links` code for an (entity_type, entity_id, action) so a QR can render — idempotent (returns existing or `created:true`). Venue-authed via `resolve_venue_caller`; ownership-checked server-side (`team` must be in one of the venue's competitions → `team_not_in_venue`; `venue` must equal the caller's venue → `not_your_venue`; action↔entity pairing enforced → `action_entity_mismatch`). Supports `team`(join_team) + `venue`(venue_landing); fixture → `unsupported_entity_type` (slice 6). INSERTs `audit_events` (`invite_link_created`) only on create (Hard Rule #9). EV-verified (idempotency + venue create + audit×2 + 5 error paths, leak 0); rpc-security-sweep PASS. **Consumers (hard-rule #14)**: `apps/venue` `InvitesView.jsx`; slice 4b reception display; slice 7 management. |
| `get_display_landing_code(p_display_token)` | `getDisplayLandingCode(displayToken)` | anon + authenticated | **Read-only** (STABLE, SECURITY DEFINER, search_path locked) — mig 252, slice 4b. Resolves the venue from `display_token` and returns its canonical `venue_landing` code + full `/q/<code>` url (`{code, url}`, both NULL if none). The reception display fetches this ONCE on mount to render the "scan to join" QR panel — kept OFF the hot `get_display_state` broadcast payload (rarely changes). Read-only: the display never creates a code (the venue provisions it via `venue_ensure_invite_link`). rpc-security-sweep PASS. **Consumers (hard-rule #14)**: `apps/display` `QRPanel.jsx`. |
| `get_venue_landing(p_venue_id)` | `getVenueLanding(venueId)` | anon + authenticated | **Read-only** (STABLE, SECURITY DEFINER, search_path locked) — mig 249, slice 3. Public "what's on at this venue" for the `/q/<venue_code>` landing. Returns `{ok, status, venue{id,name,logo_url,colours}, competitions:[{competition_id, name, status, type, format, league_code, league_name, teams:[{team_id,name,colours}]}]}`. Only `setup`/`active` competitions under the venue's `active` leagues; teams = `status='active'` (approved) ONLY — never pending or private/casual teams. `league_code` feeds the register-your-team form (`join_register_team`). Venue not found → `{ok:false, status:'not_found'}`. rpc-security-sweep PASS. **Consumers (hard-rule #14)**: `apps/inorout` `VenueLanding.jsx`. |
| `venue_owns_entity(p_venue_id, p_entity_type, p_entity_id)` | _(internal — no JS wrapper)_ | postgres/service_role only | **Internal helper** (STABLE, SECURITY DEFINER, search_path locked) — mig 254, slice 7. Boolean ownership predicate: does `entity` (`venue`/`team`/`fixture`) belong to `venue_id`? team/fixture roll up `competition_teams|fixtures → competitions → seasons → leagues.venue_id`. Called by the four management RPCs below; **explicitly revoked from anon/authenticated** (Supabase default privileges re-grant otherwise) — never client-callable. |
| `venue_list_invite_links(p_credential)` | `venueListInviteLinks(credential)` | anon + authenticated | **Read-only** (STABLE, SECURITY DEFINER, search_path locked) — mig 254, slice 7. Returns `{ok, links:[{code, entity_type, entity_id, action, label, active, use_count, max_uses, expires_at, created_at, target_name}]}` ordered active-first then newest; `target_name` server-derived (venue/team name, or "Home v Away" for fixtures). EV-verified (list-count + cross-venue isolation). **Consumers (hard-rule #14)**: `apps/venue` `InvitesView.jsx`. |
| `venue_create_invite_link(p_credential, p_entity_type, p_entity_id, p_action, p_label)` | `venueCreateInviteLink(credential, entityType, entityId, action, label)` | anon + authenticated | **Write** (VOLATILE, SECURITY DEFINER, search_path locked) — mig 254, slice 7. | `venue_set_invite_link_active(p_credential, p_code, p_active)` | `venueSetInviteLinkActive(credential, code, active)` | anon + authenticated | **Write** (VOLATILE, SECURITY DEFINER, search_path locked) — mig 254, slice 7. Toggle a code on/off. Ownership re-derived from the code's **stored** entity (never a client-passed venue) → `not_your_entity`; unknown code → `invite_link_not_found`. | `venue_repoint_invite_link(p_credential, p_code, p_entity_type, p_entity_id, p_action)` | `venueRepointInviteLink(credential, code, entityType, entityId, action)` | anon + authenticated | **Write** (VOLATILE, SECURITY DEFINER, search_path locked) — mig 254, slice 7. Re-points a code to a new destination — **fully flexible**: the new (entity_type, action) may differ from the old, so a code can move across types (team→venue→fixture). **Double ownership check**: caller must own BOTH the existing code's entity AND the new target (`not_your_entity`); new pairing enforced (`action_entity_mismatch`); unknown code → `invite_link_not_found`. INSERTs `audit_events` (`invite_link_repointed`, metadata `{from,to}`; Hard Rule #9). EV-verified (same-type + cross-type repoint + both foreign-ownership paths) + rpc-security-sweep PASS. **Consumers**: `apps/venue` `InviteLinkForm.jsx`. |

---

## SUPABASE SCHEMA CACHE

PostgREST caches function signatures. After any RPC change, cache may serve stale version.

Symptoms: 404 on a function that exists, wrong parameter order error.

Fix: `SELECT pg_notify('pgrst', 'reload schema');` in Supabase SQL editor.

---

## PITCH BOOKING RPCs (migrations 133+)

Stage 3 read RPCs (booking-owned). Write RPCs (`book_pitch_*`,
`venue_confirm_booking`, etc.) land in Stage 4; JS wrappers land with the
casual/venue UI (Stages 5/6).

| SQL function | JS wrapper | Grant | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| `search_bookable_venues(p_query)` | `searchBookableVenues(q)` | anon, authenticated | Typeahead over `venues` WHERE `bookings_enabled`+`active`**+`verification_status='verified'`** (enforcement added mig 488), name/slug/city ILIKE, LIMIT 20. Returns `[{venue_id,name,slug,city,cancellation_policy}]` (policy added mig 149). PII-free. A `pending`/`rejected` self-serve venue is now genuinely absent from public discovery until it goes live; existing operator venues default `verified` (unaffected). *Consumers: `apps/inorout` ScheduleScreen booking modal.* |
| `get_team_bookings(p_team_id)` | `getTeamBookings(teamId)` | **authenticated** | Casual read of the team's own bookings (recent + future) with venue/pitch/policy detail. Auth via `auth.uid()` → `team_admins`. Powers the in-app bookings list, live Requested→Confirmed badge, recent-venues discovery, cancel. mig 148. *Consumer: `apps/inorout` ScheduleScreen (Stage 5).* |
| `get_pitch_free_slots(p_venue_id, p_date, p_playing_area_id?, p_slot_length?)` | `getPitchFreeSlots(...)` (Stage 5) | anon, authenticated | Expands `playing_areas.booking_windows` for `p_date`'s weekday → back-to-back slots per offered length → subtracts active `pitch_occupancy`. Graceful default 08:00–22:00/60 when a pitch has no windows. Returns `[{playing_area_id,pitch_name,slot_start,slot_end,slot_minutes}]`. PII-free. *Consumers: `apps/inorout` booking modal (Stage 5).* |
| `get_pitch_occupancy(p_venue_token, p_from, p_to)` | `getPitchOccupancy(...)` (Stage 6) | anon, authenticated (token is the secret) | Venue calendar grid: one row per active occupancy row joined to fixture/booking/maintenance/**club_session/club_fixture** detail over `[p_from, p_to]`. **Returns PII** (team names, walk-in names) → venue-operator only via `resolve_venue_caller`. detail carries `kind`/`status`/`series_id` and (mig 233) **`owed`** + **`is_first`**; (mig 414) club kinds carry `title`/`team_name`/`our_team`/`opponent`/`manager_initials`. owed math via `_venue_source_owed`. **mig 414: detail now built by shared `_pitch_occupancy_detail(kind, source_id)` — output for existing kinds byte-identical (verified live).** *Consumers: `apps/venue` ScheduleGrid (icon+type word per kind, NEW badge; hard-rule #14).* |
| `get_operator_pitch_occupancy(p_venue_token, p_from, p_to)` | `getOperatorPitchOccupancy(...)` (mig 414) | anon, authenticated (token is the secret) | **NEW mig 414 (multi-venue Phase 3) — unified cross-site calendar.** Returns `{ ok, venues: [{ venue_id, venue_name, venue_address, is_self, pitches[], occupancy[] }] }` for EVERY venue the caller's operator runs (own venue + all sharing non-null `venues.company_id`). `occupancy[]` rows + `detail` are the SAME shape as `get_pitch_occupancy` (shared `_pitch_occupancy_detail`). **Returns PII** → operator only. *Consumer: `apps/venue` BookingsView ground switcher; keep per-venue shape stable for a future HQ cross-site view (hard-rule #14).* Helpers `_pitch_occupancy_detail(text,text)` + `_club_team_manager_initials(uuid)` are SECDEF, definer-only (REVOKEd anon/auth). Triggers `tg_sync_club_session_occupancy`/`tg_sync_club_fixture_occupancy` project club activity into `pitch_occupancy` + raise `slot_unavailable` on overlap (hard clash-protection, all write paths, no displacement). |

| `get_venue_resource_occupancy(p_venue_token, p_from, p_to)` | `getVenueResourceOccupancy(...)` (mig 419) | anon, authenticated (token is the secret) | **NEW mig 419 (Unified Resource Calendar Phase 1, read-only).** ONE normalised occupancy feed across **pitches + rooms (`venue_room_hires` ∪ `venue_class_sessions`) + trainers (`venue_appointments`)** for EVERY venue the operator runs (own + non-null `venues.company_id`). Returns `{ ok, venues: [{ venue_id, venue_name, is_self, pitches[], rooms[], trainers[], occupancy[] }] }`. Each `occupancy` row: `{ id, resource_type (pitch/room/trainer), resource_id, resource_name, source_kind (pitch kinds + `room_hire`/`class`/`appointment`), source_id, start, end, detail }`. Pitch rows reuse `_pitch_occupancy_detail` verbatim; new SECDEF definer-only builders `_room_occupancy_detail(text,text)` (room_hire + class; class leads with `class_name`, room is the subheading) + `_trainer_occupancy_detail(text)` (REVOKEd anon/auth). Status filter: room_hire `confirmed`/`requested`, class `scheduled`, appointment `confirmed`. **Returns PII** → operator only via `resolve_venue_caller`. Equipment is NOT here (quantity-over-time strip via `get_equipment_availability`). *Consumers (hard-rule #14): `apps/venue` BookingsView unified calendar (`ResourceCalendar` on the shared `GroupedColumnGrid` engine, Show: Pitches/Rooms/Trainers/All); Phase 2 book-from-calendar tap routing reuses this feed; keep the per-venue `{pitches,rooms,trainers,occupancy}` shape stable for a future HQ cross-site utilisation view.* |

Stage 4 write RPCs (booking-owned). Each: SECURITY DEFINER, holds/frees a
`pitch_occupancy` row through the partial EXCLUDE (taken slot → `slot_unavailable`),
audits (Phase 2 shape), broadcasts `notify_venue_change` + `notify_team_change`.
JS wrappers land with the consuming UI (Stages 5/6).

| SQL function | JS wrapper | Grant | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| `book_pitch_adhoc(p_team_id, p_playing_area_id, p_booking_date, p_kickoff_time, p_slot_minutes?)` | `bookPitchAdhoc(...)` (Stage 5) | **authenticated** | Casual one-off request. Auth via `auth.uid()` → `team_admins` (must administer `p_team_id`). Status `requested`, occupancy priority 3. Fires `booking_requested`. *Consumer: `apps/inorout` booking modal (Stage 5).* |
| `book_pitch_series(p_team_id, p_playing_area_id, p_kickoff_time, p_start_date, p_weeks, p_slot_minutes?)` | `bookPitchSeries(...)` (Stage 5) | **authenticated** | Casual block request. Creates `booking_series` + N weekly `pitch_bookings` (priority 2) atomically (any clash → `slot_unavailable`). `day_of_week` derived from `p_start_date`. Fires `booking_requested`. *Consumer: `apps/inorout` (Stage 5).* |
| `venue_create_booking(p_venue_token, p_playing_area_id, p_booking_date, p_kickoff_time, p_slot_minutes?, p_team_id?, p_booked_by_name?, p_contact_email?, p_contact_phone?)` | `venueCreateBooking(...)` (Stage 6) | anon, authenticated | Single booking → status `confirmed` directly. Team (`team_id`) OR walk-in/new (`team_id` NULL + `booked_by_name`). **Contact email + phone now REQUIRED** (mig 232 — validated via `_validate_booking_contact`; stored on `pitch_bookings.contact_email/contact_phone`). Old 7-arg signature DROPPED in mig 232. Fires `booking_confirmed`. *Consumer: `apps/venue` New-booking modal.* |
| `venue_create_booking_series(p_venue_token, p_playing_area_id, p_kickoff_time, p_start_date, p_weeks, p_team_id, p_slot_minutes?, p_contact_email?, p_contact_phone?)` | `venueCreateBookingSeries(...)` | anon, authenticated | **WRITE** (mig 232, ephemeral-verify 15/15). Venue-side weekly block: N `pitch_bookings` (kind `block`, status `confirmed`, priority-2 occupancy) under one `booking_series`, mirroring `book_pitch_series` but venue-token auth + confirmed. **Team-only** (`series_team_required` if no team); contact required; whole block rolls back on any week clash (`slot_unavailable`). Fires `booking_confirmed` (venue+team). *Consumer: `apps/venue` New-booking modal (Block).* |
| `venue_confirm_booking(p_venue_token, p_booking_id)` | `venueConfirmBooking(...)` (Stage 6; +member discount mig 277) | anon, authenticated | `requested` → `confirmed` (refuses if not pending — e.g. superseded by a fixture). Fires `booking_confirmed`. **mig 277:** applies the booker's active membership tier `discount_pct` to the charge. Member resolved by `pitch_bookings.customer_id` if set, else auto-matched by `contact_email` to an ACTIVE venue member (link then persisted). Only an active membership w/ numeric pct discounts; 100% → no charge. Returns now include `member_discount_pct`, `charge_fee_pence`; audit gains `base_fee_pence`/`member_discount_pct`/`member_customer_id`. EV 9/9 + leak 0. *Consumer: `apps/venue` requests inbox.* |
| `venue_confirm_booking_series(p_venue_token, p_series_id)` | `venueConfirmBookingSeries(...)` (mig 236; +member discount mig 277) | anon, authenticated | Confirms every still-`requested` booking in a series + mints a charge each. **mig 277:** same per-booking member discount as `venue_confirm_booking`. *Consumer: `apps/venue` requests inbox.* |
| `_booking_member_discount(p_venue_id, p_customer_id, p_email)` | — (internal helper, mig 277) | **service_role ONLY** | Returns `(customer_id, pct)` — resolves a booking's member (explicit link, else active-member email match) + clamped tier `discount_pct`. Called only inside the SECDEF confirm RPCs. |
| `venue_decline_booking(p_venue_token, p_booking_id)` | `venueDeclineBooking(...)` (Stage 6) | anon, authenticated | `requested` → `declined`, frees the slot. Fires `booking_declined`. *Consumer: `apps/venue` inbox (Stage 6).* |
| `cancel_booking(p_booking_id, p_venue_token?, p_reason?, p_note?, p_decision?, p_within_policy?)` | `cancelBooking(id, token?, opts?)` (Stage 5/6; mig 222) | anon, authenticated | Dual auth: venue token OR team admin (`auth.uid()`). Walk-ins venue-only. `requested`/`confirmed` → `cancelled`, frees slot. **mig 222:** `p_decision` `full`/`partial`/`none` acts on the booking's `venue_charges` (full→refunded, partial→due halved, none→untouched, mirrors fixture-void); reason/note/decision/refund_pence/charged_pence recorded in the `booking_cancelled` audit row; `p_within_policy` recorded only. Old 2-arg signature dropped. Returns `{ok, status, refund_pence, charged_pence}`. *Consumers: both apps; venue CancelBookingModal.* |
| `venue_list_cancellations(p_venue_token, p_limit?)` | `venueListCancellations(token, limit?)` (mig 222) | anon, authenticated | Venue read. `booking_cancelled` audit rows for this venue, newest first, joined to live pitch/team detail (reason/note/decision/refund). Rows cancelled pre-mig-222 have null detail. *Consumers: venue CancellationsLog + CSV export.* |
| `venue_list_customers(p_venue_token)` | `venueListCustomers(token)` (mig 223) | anon, authenticated | Venue read, **venue-domain only**. Bookers at this venue (teams grouped by `team_id`, walk-ins by `booked_by_name`) aggregated from `pitch_bookings` + `venue_charges` (+ `venue_payments` for collected): bookings_count, total_paid/outstanding pence, recency-based `nudge_status` (new/healthy/lapsing/dormant). No casual `players`/`team_admins`/ins read — respects the venue↔casual RLS wall. *Consumers: venue CustomersView.* |
| `venue_request_nudge(p_venue_token, p_booker_key, p_template?)` | `venueRequestNudge(token, bookerKey, template?)` (mig 224) | anon, authenticated | Fire-and-forget write. Records a `venue_nudge_requested` audit_event for a **team** booker at this venue (authorizes via a booking match). Returns `{ok, recipients}` (count only — no contact exposed) or `{ok:false, reason:'no_contact'}` (walk-ins / no admin email). **Delivery is server-side:** `cron.js onboardingEmailJob` resolves the team admin email (`teamAdminEmails`) and sends the `venue_nudge` mailer template — the venue never sees the address. Email live; SMS/WhatsApp no-op till Twilio keys. *Consumers: venue CustomersView NudgeModal; sender = apps/inorout/api/cron.js.* |
| `venue_get_booking_ins(p_venue_token)` | `venueGetBookingIns(token)` (mig 225) | anon, authenticated | Venue read, **cross-domain by opt-in** (counts only). No player identities cross to the venue. *Consumers: venue ScheduleGrid/DayAgenda/BookingDetailModal.* |

| **Phase 7 Stripe scaffolding (mig 279 — DORMANT, no money moves; see DECISIONS money-flow gate)** | | | |

| **Class-package precedence (mig 344):** `_apply_class_booking_charge` re-issued with a **waiver > package > charge** order — a waived session (tier `included_sessions`/`first_session_free`/£0) never burns a paid credit; else a valid balance (soonest-expiring, `FOR UPDATE`) is decremented and the booking marked `payment_status='paid'`,`package_balance_id=<bal>` with NO charge; else the normal `class` charge. `member_cancel_class_booking` re-issued: restores the credit (`+1`) on cancel within cutoff (`credit_restored` in return + audit). `venue_cancel_class_session`/`_series` re-issued: restore burned credits for every cancelled booking (a venue cancel must not strand member money). Return shapes otherwise unchanged (Hard Rule #7). |

Self-serve hire request. Calls `_space_is_available` → `{ok:false,reason:'space_unavailable'}` on overlap (with class sessions OR other live hires); per-member open-request throttle → `'too_many_requests'`. Creates `venue_room_hires` `booker_type='member'` status `requested`; links optional equipment add-ons as `requested` `equipment_bookings` (only venue's own kit, no charge). Queues `room_hire_requested` ack. Audit `room_hire_requested` (`actor_type='player'`). *Consumer: `apps/inorout` VenueLanding (HireSpace).* |
| `public_enquire_room_hire(p_space_id, p_name, p_email, p_phone, p_starts_at, p_ends_at, p_purpose, p_attendee_count?)` | `publicEnquireRoomHire(spaceId, {name,email,phone,startsAt,endsAt,purpose,attendeeCount})` | **anon, authenticated** | **WRITE — FIRST anon write in this epic** (mig 342). Restricted to `is_enquiry_only` spaces (`not_enquiry_only` reject); no charge; validates + length-caps name(120)/email(160)/phone(40)/purpose(500) (`name_required`/`bad_email`/`purpose_required`/`input_too_long`); per-email+space 10-min throttle → `'too_many_requests'`. Creates `booker_type='non_member'` `requested`. Queues `room_hire_requested` ack. Audit `room_hire_enquired` **`actor_type='system'`, `actor_user_id=NULL`** (anon-safe — the whitelist has no `anon`). Returns only `{ok, hire_id}` (no venue internals). *Consumer: VenueLanding (HireSpace contact form).* |
| `venue_list_room_hires(p_venue_token, p_status?)` | `venueListRoomHires(token, status?)` | anon, authenticated (token-resolved) | **READ** (mig 342). STABLE. Caller's hires (optional status filter), requests first then by `starts_at`; each row + space name/type, booker, latest `charge_status`, and `equipment[]` add-ons (joined `equipment_bookings`+`equipment`). *Consumer: `apps/venue` RoomHiresView.* |
| `venue_confirm_room_hire(p_venue_token, p_hire_id, p_price_pence, p_deposit_pence?)` | `venueConfirmRoomHire(token, hireId, pricePence, depositPence?)` | anon, authenticated (token-resolved) | **WRITE** (mig 342). `requested`→`confirmed`; prices it; raises a `venue_charges` row `source_type='room_hire'`,`source_id=hire_id::text`,`status='unpaid'` (if price>0; idempotent vs non-refunded); confirms linked equipment add-ons; notifies booker (`room_hire_confirmed`). `not_confirmable`/`bad_price`/`hire_not_found`/`invalid_venue_token`. Audit `room_hire_confirmed`. *Consumer: RoomHiresView.* |
| `venue_cancel_room_hire(p_venue_token, p_hire_id, p_reason?)` | `venueCancelRoomHire(token, hireId, reason?)` | anon, authenticated (token-resolved) | **WRITE** (mig 342). status→`cancelled`; refunds the `room_hire` charge (`status='refunded'`); cancels linked equipment add-ons; a `held` deposit → `returned`; notifies booker (`room_hire_cancelled`). Idempotent (`{ok,already}`). Returns `{ok, refunded, deposit_status}`. Audit `room_hire_cancelled`. *Consumer: RoomHiresView.* |
| `venue_record_hire_deposit(p_venue_token, p_hire_id, p_deposit_status)` | `venueRecordHireDeposit(token, hireId, depositStatus)` | anon, authenticated (token-resolved) | **WRITE** (mig 342). Transitions `deposit_status` ∈ none/held/returned/forfeited (`bad_deposit_status` otherwise). Row-tracked — no separate ledger row (mirrors equipment-hire deposits). Audit `room_hire_deposit_recorded`. *Consumer: RoomHiresView.* |
| `venue_create_room_hire(p_venue_token, p_space_id, p_starts_at, p_ends_at, p_purpose, p_price_pence?, p_booker_name?, p_booker_email?, p_booker_phone?, p_deposit_pence?, p_attendee_count?, p_member_profile_id?)` | `venueCreateRoomHire(token, spaceId, startsAt, endsAt, purpose, {pricePence?, bookerName?, bookerEmail?, bookerPhone?, depositPence?, attendeeCount?, memberProfileId?})` | anon, authenticated (token-resolved) | **WRITE** (mig 423, calendar Phase 2b, EV 13/13 + leak 0, rpc-security PASS). Operator ad-hoc room hire **straight to `confirmed`** (operator is the authority — mirrors `venue_create_equipment_hire`/walk-in). Booker = a member (`p_member_profile_id` → `booker_type='member'`, contact pulled from profile but overridable) OR a walk-in (`p_booker_name` → `non_member`; `booker_required` if neither). **Clash: REUSES `_space_is_available` under a `SELECT … FOR UPDATE` lock on the `venue_spaces` row** (no hard EXCLUDE — soft guard + lock). Space ownership-checked → `space_not_in_venue`. Raises a `room_hire` `venue_charges` row (unpaid) if price>0; notifies booker (`room_hire_confirmed`). `purpose_required`/`bad_time_range`/`bad_price`/`space_unavailable`/`invalid_venue_token`. Audit `room_hire_created_by_operator`. *Consumer: `apps/venue` BookingsView unified calendar → RoomHireModal (room-lane tap → chooser).* |
| `venue_create_appointment(p_venue_token, p_trainer_id, p_member_profile_id, p_starts_at, p_ends_at?, p_price_pence?)` | `venueCreateAppointment(token, trainerId, memberProfileId, startsAt, {endsAt?, pricePence?})` | anon, authenticated (token-resolved) | **WRITE** (mig 423, calendar Phase 2b, EV 13/13 + leak 0, rpc-security PASS). Operator books an **EXISTING member** (member_profile_id is NOT NULL on `venue_appointments`; no walk-in PT v1) into a trainer slot, **straight to `confirmed`**. **No availability-window enforcement (ad-hoc override)** — window check stays member-side. `ends` defaults to the trainer's `default_session_minutes`, price to the trainer's `price_pence`. **Clash: inlined overlap guard vs non-cancelled `venue_appointments` (the `UNIQUE(trainer_id, starts_at)` index only catches an exact-start collision) → `{ok:false, reason:'slot_taken'}`; unique index is the backstop.** Trainer ownership-checked under a row lock → `trainer_not_in_venue`. Raises a `pt` `venue_charges` row (unpaid) if price>0. `member_not_found`/`slot_in_past`/`bad_time_range`/`bad_price`/`invalid_venue_token`. Audit `appointment_created_by_operator`. *Consumer: `apps/venue` BookingsView unified calendar → AppointmentModal (trainer-lane tap).* |
| `member_list_hireable_spaces(p_venue_id)` | `memberListHireableSpaces(venueId)` | **anon, authenticated** | **READ** (mig 342). Active spaces for a venue + `is_enquiry_only` + enquiry contact — powers the public "Hire a space" cards. *Consumer: VenueLanding (HireSpace).* |
| `member_list_my_room_hires(p_venue_id?)` | `memberListMyRoomHires(venueId?)` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **READ** (mig 342). `auth.uid()`→`member_profiles`; the caller's hires (optional venue scope) + `is_upcoming` flag. Gated **manage_memberships OR manage_facility**. `contact_kind` derived from `team_kind`: **league → a `venue_customers` person** (validated in-venue, not erased); **club → an active manager/assistant/coach of THAT team** (`club_team_managers`, else `contact_not_team_staff`). ## OPS / INTERNAL CRON RPCs (no JS wrapper — called directly from api/cron.js)

| SQL function | Grant | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| `expire_staff_dbs()` | service_role only (anon + authenticated **revoked explicitly** — Supabase auto-grants both; requires manual REVOKE in mig 305) | **Migration 305.** **WRITE.** UPDATE `club_staff_dbs` SET status='expired' WHERE status='valid' AND expiry_date < CURRENT_DATE. Returns `{expired: int}`. SECURITY DEFINER, `search_path=public`. No JS wrapper — called via `supabase.rpc()` directly in `api/cron.js` `dbsExpiryJob` (08:00 UK, time-window guard 15min). *Consumer: `apps/inorout/api/cron.js` only.* |
| `get_ops_usage_digest(p_from date, p_to date, p_prev_from date?, p_prev_to date?)` | service_role only (anon + authenticated **revoked**) | **Migration 234.** STABLE, read-only. Operator-only "is the casual app being used?" analytics over a window `[p_from,p_to]` (UK dates, inclusive) + an optional previous window for the wk/wk delta. Returns one jsonb: `squads{total,active,new[]}`, `players{total,new,disabled_now,disabled_in_window,deleted_in_window}`, `activity{total_events,app_opens,active_players,availability_marks,bookings,by_action[]}`, `dormancy[{id,name,last_active,days_since}]`, `prev{total_events,active_players}`. **Real squads only** — demo (`team_demo%`) AND demo-company league seed (`team_dc%`) stripped in SQL per Hard Rule #15, so the numbers are genuine onboarded squads. SECURITY DEFINER, `search_path=public`. No JS wrapper — called via `supabase.rpc()` directly in `api/cron.js` (same pattern as `hq_get_analytics_for_company`/`weeklyDigestJob`), so it never lands in `packages/core`. **Consumers (Hard Rule #14)**: `api/cron.js` `opsDailyDigestJob` (Tue–Sun 08:00 UK, previous day) + `opsWeeklyDigestJob` (Mon 08:00 UK, previous week) → `_mailer.js` `opsDailyDigest`/`opsWeeklyDigest` templates → `OPS_DIGEST_EMAIL` (defaults to operator address); **planned**: Phase 7 Gaffer AI-narration layer reads this same shape for the prose digest. Return-shape changes must check both cron.js templates AND that future consumer. |

| `_advance_tournament_winner(p_fixture_id)` | *(internal — no JS wrapper)* | **REVOKED from PUBLIC, anon, authenticated** (postgres + service_role only) | **WRITE (mig 324, internal helper).** Called from `ref_confirm_tournament_match` on every knockout FT confirmation. Derives winner (home_score > away_score; draws = no-op). Slots winner into the next-round fixture via `knockout_home_feeder_id`/`knockout_away_feeder_id` self-referential FKs. Promotes that fixture to `status='scheduled'` once both home + away slots filled. No audit entry (called from within an audited RPC). *Consumer: ref_confirm_tournament_match only.* |
| `club_admin_seed_knockout(p_tournament_event_id, p_competition_id)` | `clubAdminSeedKnockout(tournamentEventId, competitionId)` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **WRITE (mig 324, EV 10/10).** Auth: auth.uid()→member_profiles→club_team_managers. Guards: all group-stage fixtures must be `completed`; total qualifiers (top 2 per group, rank=1+2) must be a power of 2 (2/4/8/16); `competition.config.knockout_seeded` must be false. Stamps `competition_teams.group_rank` via H2H tiebreaker (same Phase 7A CTE). Collects qualifiers ordered by rank then group_label. Seeds bracket serpentine (seed[i] vs seed[n-i+1]) guaranteeing cross-group R1. Round-1 fixtures: teams populated, `status='scheduled'`. Future-round fixtures: teams NULL, `knockout_home/away_feeder_id` set, `status='allocated'`. Round names from ['Final','Semi-Finals','Quarter-Finals','Round of 16']. Sets `competitions.config.knockout_seeded=true`. Audit `tournament_knockout_seeded`. Returns `{ok, total_qualifiers, knockout_rounds}`. Errors: `not_authenticated`, `not_authorised`, `tournament_not_found`, `competition_not_found`, `knockout_already_seeded`, `incomplete_group_fixtures`, `no_groups_found`, `bracket_size_not_supported`. *Consumer: SessionsScreen "Advance to Knockout" button (director view).* |

| **Phase 7D — Event OS: Double Elimination (mig 325, session 128). | `_advance_tournament_double_elim(p_fixture_id)` | *(internal — no JS wrapper)* | **REVOKED from PUBLIC, anon, authenticated** (postgres + service_role only) | **WRITE (mig 325, internal helper).** Called from `ref_confirm_tournament_match` when `fixture.de_bracket IS NOT NULL`. Derives winner/loser (home_score > away_score; draws = no-op). Winner → slotted via feeder mechanism into next WB/LB/GF fixture. Loser → slotted via `de_loser_to_fixture_id`/`de_loser_to_slot` into LB. Fixture promoted to `scheduled` once both slots filled. *Consumer: ref_confirm_tournament_match only.* |
| `club_admin_seed_double_elimination(p_tournament_event_id, p_competition_id)` | `clubAdminSeedDoubleElimination(tournamentEventId, competitionId)` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **WRITE (mig 325, EV 15/15).** Auth: auth.uid()→member_profiles→club_team_managers. Guards: power-of-2 active teams (4/8/16); `competition.config.knockout_seeded` must be false. Builds full bracket: WB R1 seeded pairs (seed[i] vs seed[n-i+1]) + `de_loser_to_fixture_id` wiring to LB R1 (`de_loser_to_slot` = home for first, away for second). Loop WB R2..k: drop round (home_feeder=LB consolidation winner, away via `de_loser_to_fixture_id` of WB round loser) + consolidation round (LB survivors). Grand Final: home_feeder=WB Final, away_feeder=LB Final. Sets `competitions.config.knockout_seeded=true`. Audit `tournament_de_seeded`. Returns `{ok, total_teams, wb_fixtures, lb_fixtures}`. Errors: `not_enough_teams`, `already_seeded`. *Consumer: SessionsScreen "Seed double elimination" button (director view, format=double_elimination).* |

| `club_admin_remove_sponsor(p_sponsor_id)` | `clubAdminRemoveSponsor(sponsorId)` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **WRITE (mig 327).** Ownership guard: sponsor → tournament_events.club_id → club_team_managers. Hard-deletes from `tournament_sponsors`. Audit `tournament_sponsor_removed`. *Consumer: SessionsScreen Sponsors section.* |
| `club_admin_set_branding(p_tournament_event_id, p_primary_colour?, p_secondary_colour?, p_custom_logo_url?)` | `clubAdminSetBranding(tournamentEventId, {primaryColour, secondaryColour, customLogoUrl})` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **WRITE (mig 327).** Writes into `tournament_events.branding` jsonb (column from mig 315). Keys: `primary_colour`, `secondary_colour`, `custom_logo_url` (all nullable text). Audit `tournament_branding_updated`. *Consumer: SessionsScreen Branding section.* |
| `club_admin_set_player_of_tournament(p_tournament_event_id, p_name, p_team_name?)` | `clubAdminSetPlayerOfTournament(tournamentEventId, name, teamName?)` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **WRITE (mig 327).** name_required guard. Updates `tournament_events.player_of_tournament_name` + `_team`. Audit `tournament_pot_set`. *Consumer: SessionsScreen Player of Tournament section.* |
| `club_admin_get_equipment_for_tournament(p_tournament_event_id)` | `clubAdminGetEquipmentForTournament(tournamentEventId)` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **READ (mig 327).** Returns active equipment catalogue at the tournament's venue (`equipment.active=true` for that `venue_id`). Rows: `{equipment_id, name, category, quantity, default_fee_pence, deposit_pence, hire_unit, condition}`. *Consumer: SessionsScreen Equipment section catalogue picker.* |
| `club_admin_book_equipment_for_tournament(p_tournament_event_id, p_equipment_id, p_qty, p_start_at, p_end_at, p_due_back_at?)` | `clubAdminBookEquipmentForTournament(tournamentEventId, equipmentId, qty, startAt, endAt, dueBackAt?)` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **WRITE (mig 327).** invalid_quantity / invalid_window guards. Availability check via `_equipment_peak_committed`. Creates `equipment_bookings` row at `status='confirmed'` linked via `tournament_event_id`. No venue_charges row (directors don't bill through venue — staff handle). Audit `tournament_equipment_booked`. Returns `{ok, booking_id}`. *Consumer: SessionsScreen Equipment section booking form.* |
| `club_admin_list_tournament_equipment_bookings(p_tournament_event_id)` | `clubAdminListTournamentEquipmentBookings(tournamentEventId)` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **READ (mig 327).** Returns active (not cancelled/declined) bookings for a tournament. Rows: `{booking_id, equipment_id, equipment_name, category, qty, start_at, end_at, due_back_at, returned_at, status, amount_pence}`. **Field is `qty`, not `qty_booked`.** *Consumer: SessionsScreen Equipment section bookings list.* |
| `club_admin_cancel_equipment_booking(p_booking_id)` | `clubAdminCancelEquipmentBooking(bookingId)` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **WRITE (mig 327).** Ownership guard: booking → tournament_event_id → tournament_events.club_id → club_team_managers. cannot_cancel guard for `status IN ('out','returned','cancelled')`. Sets `status='cancelled'`. Audit `tournament_equipment_booking_cancelled`. *Consumer: SessionsScreen Equipment section cancel button.* |
| `get_tournament_public(p_slug)` | `getTournamentPublic(slug)` | **anon, authenticated** | **READ (mig 317; … mig 326; extended mig 327).** **Mig 327 adds:** `branding {primary_colour, secondary_colour, custom_logo_url}`, `sponsors[]`, `player_of_tournament_name`, `player_of_tournament_team`. *Consumer: apps/inorout TournamentScreen — branding header, sponsor strip, POT trophy card.* |
| `club_admin_get_tournament(p_slug)` | `clubAdminGetTournament(slug)` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **READ (mig 316; extended mig 318, mig 324; extended mig 327).** **Mig 327 adds:** `sponsors[]`, `player_of_tournament_name`, `player_of_tournament_team`. *Consumer: SessionsScreen Tournaments tab expand panel.* |

### Modular Platform Epic B — public club home page (mig 445)

The anon public-read behind `/c/<slug>` (the "Pitchero destroyer" club page). SECDEF, search_path locked, single overload, `REVOKE ALL FROM public` then GRANT anon+authenticated. Read-only (no audit). Clones `get_tournament_public`'s grant pattern + `get_club_league_public`'s fixtures logic. Hard Rule #14 — consumer recorded so a later return-shape change can't silently break the Phase 4 UI.

| RPC (SQL) | JS wrapper | grants | description |
|---|---|---|---|
| `get_club_public(p_slug)` | `getClubPublic(slug)` | **anon, authenticated** | **READ (mig 445), SECDEF.** Keyed on `club_pages.slug`; returns `{found:false}` when missing OR `published=false`. On success: `{found:true, club{id,name,short_name,discipline,founded_year}, branding{primary/secondary/accent_colour,crest_url,hero_url,tagline,about,socials,sections}, teams[cohort{…,teams[{…,members[]}]}], leagues[{league_id,name,season_label,fixtures[]}], sponsors[] (active, by display_order), news[] (status='published', newest first), tournaments[] (this club's non-draft events — the hub link)}`. **No standings table** — external `club_fixtures` (free-text opponents, our games only) can't yield one; the live FA table is the P4 `fa_embed_code` iframe. **Safeguarding applied SERVER-SIDE** from `clubs.safeguarding_config`: `min_public_age` (int, default 18), `hide_public_rosters` (bool, default false). Minors (or unknown DOB) → first name + surname initial, `photo_url` null (no member photo column exists yet — gate lands when one is added); adults shown in full. ***Consumer: apps/inorout Phase 4 `ClubPublicScreen.jsx` (`/c/<slug>`) — currently a JSON-dump stub.*** EV 8/8 + leak-0. |

### watchOS companion — identity layer (mig 369)

Net-new ref/official identity. **Primary consumer = the watchOS companion app** (supabase-swift calls these RPCs directly; the JS wrappers serve the web admin surfaces). Hard Rule #14 — record the watch consumer now so a later return-shape change can't silently break it; Hard Rule #12 — `get_my_next_assignment`'s shape is LOCKED for Swift `CodingKeys`.

| RPC (SQL) | JS wrapper | grants | description |
|---|---|---|---|
| `get_my_next_assignment(p_role_filter?)` | `getMyNextAssignment(roleFilter?)` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **READ/resolver (mig 369), SECDEF STABLE.** `auth.uid()` → next relevant game across the **fixture arm** (`match_officials.user_id`→`fixtures.official_id`→`ref_token`; covers league + club-cohort fixtures) + **casual arm** (`players.user_id`→`matches.ref_player_id`→`matches.ref_token`). Tie-break **in-progress > soonest kickoff > role priority (league=1, casual=2)**. **LOCKED return shape:** `{ ok, game_count, next: <game|null>, games: [<game>…] }`; game = `{ context('league'|'casual'), role, ref_token, game_id, kickoff_at, status, is_in_progress, venue_name, home_team, away_team, squad_name }`. `p_role_filter ∈ {null,'league','casual'}`. *Consumer: watchOS home screen + "you have N games" chooser.* |
| `ref_link_self_to_official()` | `refLinkSelfToOfficial()` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **WRITE (mig 369), SECDEF.** Self-claim: links EVERY `match_officials` card whose `email` = the caller's verified `auth.users.email` and `user_id IS NULL` → `auth.uid()`. One human → many venue cards. Audit `official_self_linked` per card. Returns `{ ok, linked_count, official_ids[] }`. *Consumer: watchOS sign-in + Settings.* |
| `venue_link_official_to_user(p_venue_token, p_official_id, p_email)` | `venueLinkOfficialToUser(venueToken, officialId, email)` | **anon, authenticated** | **WRITE (mig 369), SECDEF.** Operator-bind: sets `match_officials.user_id` to whichever auth user owns `p_email` (official must be in caller's venue). No account for that email → `{ok:false, reason:'no_account_for_email'}` (card unchanged). Audit `official_linked_by_operator`. *Consumer: venue dashboard officials screen.* |
| `assign_casual_match_ref(p_admin_token, p_match_id, p_player_id)` | `assignCasualMatchRef(adminToken, matchId, playerId)` | **anon, authenticated** | **WRITE (mig 369), SECDEF.** Squad admin assigns a squad member as the match's ref (per-game, changeable; `p_player_id=null` clears). Mints `matches.ref_token` on first assignment (kept stable; drives nothing until Phase 5). Guards: `invalid_admin_token` / `match_not_found` / `match_not_in_team` / `player_not_in_team`. Audit `casual_ref_assigned`/`_changed`/`_cleared`. Returns `{ ok, match_id, ref_player_id, ref_token }`. *Consumer: inorout admin match UI ref-slot toggle (later cycle) + watchOS casual arm.* |
| `club_admin_assign_cohort_official(p_venue_token, p_cohort_id, p_official_id)` | `clubAdminAssignCohortOfficial(venueToken, cohortId, officialId)` | **anon, authenticated** | **WRITE (mig 369), SECDEF.** Sets a cohort's `primary_official_id` (default-official convenience; caller's venue must be in the cohort's club via `club_venues`; `null` clears). Guards: `invalid_venue_token` / `cohort_not_found` / `cohort_not_in_venue` / `official_unavailable`. Audit `cohort_official_assigned`/`_changed`/`_cleared`. *Consumer: venue dashboard cohort screen.* |

### watchOS companion — Phase 5, casual ref writes (mig 471)

No JS wrappers yet (backend/schema only — no frontend wiring this phase; **primary consumer = the watchOS companion app** via supabase-swift, Hard Rule #14). All token-gated via `matches.ref_token` (mirrors the league `ref_*` RPCs' `_ref_resolve_fixture` pattern) — **anon, authenticated** grants. All idempotent via `p_client_event_id uuid` (`ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`, matches the league `client_event_id` engine, mig 120). New table `casual_match_events` — parallel to `match_events` (league), shaped for casual: `team_assignment CHECK IN ('A','B')` instead of a `teams.id` FK (a casual match is one team's squad split into scrimmage sides, no second team row to FK to), `match_id text → matches.id` instead of `fixture_id`. RLS enabled, no public policies (RPC-only).

| RPC (SQL) | grants | description |
|---|---|---|
| `casual_ref_start_match(p_ref_token, p_client_event_id, p_local_timestamp?)` | anon, authenticated | **WRITE (mig 471), SECDEF.** Sets `matches.ref_started_at` (idempotent, kept stable on replay) + logs a `kickoff` event. Guards: `invalid_ref_token` / `match_already_resulted`. |
| `casual_ref_record_goal(p_ref_token, p_player_id, p_minute, p_period, p_client_event_id, p_own_goal?, p_local_timestamp?)` | anon, authenticated | **WRITE (mig 471), SECDEF.** Logs a goal/own-goal event only — **does not touch `player_match.goals` or `matches.score_a/score_b`**; the admin's existing end-of-match confirm flow (mig 013) stays the sole writer of final goals, unchanged. Side (A/B) derived server-side from `matches.teams_draft` (pre-confirm roster — `team_a`/`team_b` are NULL until the admin confirms). Guards: `player_not_in_match`. |
| `casual_ref_record_card(p_ref_token, p_player_id, p_minute, p_period, p_colour, p_client_event_id, p_local_timestamp?)` | anon, authenticated | **WRITE (mig 471), SECDEF.** Logs a yellow/red card event only (counted into `player_match` at full-time, not incremented here — see `casual_ref_confirm_full_time`). Guards: `invalid_card_colour` / `player_not_in_match`. |
| `casual_ref_record_substitution(p_ref_token, p_on_player_id, p_off_player_id, p_minute, p_period, p_client_event_id, p_local_timestamp?)` | anon, authenticated | **WRITE (mig 471), SECDEF.** Logs a substitution event (log only — no `player_match` aggregate for subs). Guards: `missing_substitution_players` / `substitution_side_mismatch`. |
| `casual_ref_record_sin_bin(p_ref_token, p_player_id, p_minute, p_period, p_duration_minutes, p_client_event_id, p_local_timestamp?)` | anon, authenticated | **WRITE (mig 471), SECDEF.** Logs a sin-bin event with `duration` (minutes) — no `player_match` column exists for sin-bins, log only. Guards: `invalid_sin_bin_duration` / `player_not_in_match`. |
| `casual_ref_set_period(p_ref_token, p_period, p_client_event_id, p_local_timestamp?)` | anon, authenticated | **WRITE (mig 471), SECDEF.** Logs a `period_change` event (`p_period ∈ {'HT','2H'}`). Guards: `invalid_period`. |
| `casual_ref_undo_event(p_ref_token, p_client_event_id)` | anon, authenticated | **WRITE (mig 471), SECDEF.** Deletes the matching event row by `client_event_id` (plain delete — no aggregate to reverse, since cards are derived by `COUNT()` at full-time, not incremented per-tap). Returns `{ok:true, noop:true}` if already gone/never existed. |
| `casual_ref_confirm_full_time(p_ref_token)` | anon, authenticated | **WRITE (mig 471), SECDEF.** The ONLY writer of `player_match.yellow_cards`/`red_cards`/`own_goals` (Phase-3 columns, previously unwritten by any RPC — first-ever writer, zero regression risk). Derives each carded/own-goal player's counts from `casual_match_events` via `COUNT()` and upserts `player_match` (creating the row early from `teams_draft` if the admin hasn't confirmed the result yet). Idempotent — safe to call more than once, recomputes rather than increments. **Does not touch `goals`/`result`/`motm`/`had_bibs`/`attended`/`team_assignment` on an existing row** (verified against mig 013's `ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE` column list — the admin's later confirm-result RPC owns those, disjoint column sets, no collision). Guard: `match_not_started`. |

Consumers: the watchOS companion app (Phase 5, still App-Store-gated for the native build) — see [[project_watchos_companion]] / DECISIONS.md #11 (watchOS s161 decisions) for the full design rationale.

### Unified Identity & Sync Spine — Phase 0b resolvers (mig 372)

The one "my world" resolver + the shared ref-assignment list. All three are SECDEF, **STABLE / read-only** (no writes, no `audit_events`), **authenticated-only** (anon REVOKED), keyed on the canonical `person_id` (mig 371) derived from `auth.uid()` via `people.auth_user_id` (1:1, so equivalent-or-better than the old `user_id` joins; resolves empty for a user with no `people` row). Hard Rule #14 — consumers recorded so a later return-shape change can't silently break a downstream surface. Hard Rule #12 — `get_my_next_assignment`'s shape stays LOCKED (Swift `CodingKeys`).

| RPC (SQL) | JS wrapper | grants | description |
|---|---|---|---|
| `get_my_assignments(p_role_filter?)` | `getMyAssignments(roleFilter?)` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **READ/resolver (mig 372), SECDEF STABLE.** THE shared ref list — lifts mig 369's two arms (fixture/OFFICIAL `match_officials.person_id`→`fixtures.official_id`→`ref_token`; casual/PLAYER `players.person_id`→`matches.ref_player_id`→`matches.ref_token`), now person-keyed. Same per-game shape as `get_my_next_assignment`. Tie-break in-progress > soonest kickoff > role priority (league=1, casual=2). Returns `{ ok, game_count, games: [<game>…] }`. `p_role_filter ∈ {null,'league','casual'}`. ***Consumers: apps/ref logged-in "my fixtures" list (replaces per-token-only entry) + watchOS companion.*** |
| `get_my_officiating_history(p_limit?)` | `getMyOfficiatingHistory(limit?)` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **READ/resolver (mig 441; tournament arm added mig 455), SECDEF STABLE, read-only (no audit).** The PAST counterpart to `get_my_assignments` — completed games this person officiated, for the read-only "Past" section in RefFixtures. THREE person-keyed arms, all TERMINAL only (league: `fixtures.status='completed'`, sides → `teams`; casual: `matches.winner IS NOT NULL`; **tournament (mig 455): `fixtures.status='completed' AND home_competition_team_id IS NOT NULL`, sides → `competition_teams`, `context='tournament'`, venue via playing_area→tournament_event→official COALESCE — mirrors mig 443's `get_my_tournament_assignments`**). No overlap: the league arm INNER-JOINs `teams ON home_team_id` (NULL for tournament fixtures), so tournament rows are additive, never double-counted. Per-game shape = `get_my_assignments`'s shape PLUS `home_score`/`away_score`, `is_in_progress` always false — identical across all three arms (UNION ALL). Most-recent-first (`kickoff_at DESC`), capped at `p_limit` (default 50, clamped 1–200). Returns `{ ok, game_count, games: [<game>…] }`. Tapping a row reuses the RefMatch overlay → `/ref/<ref_token>`; the ref app routes `completed → PostMatch` so it opens read-only. SEPARATE from the Swift-locked `get_my_assignments` — never folded in. ***Consumer: apps/inorout RefFixtures.jsx (Past section) — renders all three contexts via the unchanged `PastRow`, no frontend change.*** |
| `get_my_tournament_assignments()` | `getMyTournamentAssignments()` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **READ/resolver (mig 443, Referee PR #4), SECDEF STABLE, read-only.** The TOURNAMENT arm — a SEPARATE parallel reader to the Swift-locked `get_my_assignments` (mig 372 stays untouched). Person-keyed exactly like mig 372 (`match_officials.person_id`→`fixtures.official_id`) but for Event OS fixtures (`home_competition_team_id IS NOT NULL`); team names from `competition_teams`, venue from playing-area→tournament_event→official COALESCE. IDENTICAL per-game shape with `context='tournament'`, live + upcoming only. Returns `{ ok, game_count, games:[<game>…] }`. Merged client-side in RefFixtures (live first, soonest kickoff). Also folded into `get_my_world().ref_assignments` (mig 443) so a tournament-ONLY ref resolves the `referee` role in nav.js. ***Consumer: apps/inorout RefFixtures.jsx (tournament rows, "Cup" chip).*** |
| `get_my_next_assignment(p_role_filter?)` | `getMyNextAssignment(roleFilter?)` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **READ/resolver — REWRITTEN mig 372 as a THIN WRAPPER over `get_my_assignments` (`next = games[0]`).** LOCKED return shape unchanged: `{ ok, game_count, next: <game|null>, games: [<game>…] }`; game = `{ context('league'|'casual'), role, ref_token, game_id, kickoff_at, status, is_in_progress, venue_name, home_team, away_team, squad_name }`. EV-proven `next ≡ games[0]`. ***Consumer: watchOS home screen + "you have N games" chooser.*** |
| `ref_respond_to_assignment(p_context, p_game_id, p_response)` | `refRespondToAssignment(context, gameId, response)` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **WRITE (mig 442, Referee PR #3), SECDEF.** A ref accepts/declines a specific assignment. `context ∈ league\|casual`, `response ∈ accepted\|declined`. Verifies the caller's person (`auth.uid()`→`people`) is the CURRENTLY-assigned official (league: `fixtures.official_id`→`match_officials.person_id`, status non-terminal) or `ref_player` (casual: `matches.ref_player_id`→`players.person_id`, `winner IS NULL`), else `not_your_assignment`. Upserts `ref_assignment_responses` (unique `context,game_id,person_id` → a re-assignment to a different ref reads "pending"; no reset logic). Audit `ref_assignment_accepted\|_declined` (Hard Rule #9), team_id = `match_officials.venue_id` (league) / `matches.team_id` (casual). Guards `invalid_context\|invalid_response\|game_id_required\|no_person`. Returns `{ ok, context, game_id, response }`. EV-proven (incl. 5 error-paths + unauth). **Mig 443 (Referee PR #4): `context` now also accepts `'tournament'`** (CHECK on `ref_assignment_responses` extended to `league\|casual\|tournament`; new tournament arm resolves the same league way but `home_competition_team_id IS NOT NULL`). ***Consumers: apps/inorout RefFixtures (ref, league+casual+tournament), apps/venue surface (operator read).*** |
| `ref_add_unavailability(p_start, p_end, p_note?)` | `refAddUnavailability(start, end, note?)` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **WRITE (mig 442, Referee PR #3), SECDEF.** Ref adds a blackout date range (`ref_unavailability`, person-keyed). Guards `dates_required\|end_before_start\|no_person`; note trimmed→NULL if blank. Audit `ref_unavailability_added` (team_id = `ref_person:<person>`). Returns `{ ok, id, start_date, end_date }`. EV-proven. ***Consumer: apps/inorout RefFixtures "My availability".*** |
| `ref_remove_unavailability(p_id)` | `refRemoveUnavailability(id)` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **WRITE (mig 442, Referee PR #3), SECDEF.** Deletes one of the caller's OWN `ref_unavailability` rows (`person_id = person of auth.uid()`); `not_found` if it isn't theirs. Audit `ref_unavailability_removed`. Returns `{ ok, removed_id }`. EV-proven. ***Consumer: apps/inorout RefFixtures.*** |
| `get_my_ref_status()` | `getMyRefStatus()` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **READ (mig 442, Referee PR #3), SECDEF STABLE, read-only.** The caller's own ref state, merged client-side into RefFixtures (the Swift-locked `get_my_assignments` stays untouched). Returns `{ ok, responses:[{context, game_id, response, responded_at}…], unavailability:[{id, start_date, end_date, note}… (end_date≥today, soonest first)] }`. ***Consumer: apps/inorout RefFixtures (accept/decline state + availability list).*** |
| `venue_get_ref_responses(p_venue_token)` | `venueGetRefResponses(venueToken)` | **anon + authenticated** (venue-token) | **READ (mig 442, Referee PR #3), SECDEF STABLE, read-only.** Operator surface (LEAGUE only). Resolves the venue via `resolve_venue_caller`. Returns `{ ok, fixture_responses:[{fixture_id, official_id, response, responded_at}… — only fixtures WITH a response; pending omitted], official_unavailability:[{official_id, start_date, end_date}… — the venue's officials, end_date≥today] }`. Merged into venue dashboard state → FixtureCard ref-response chip + FixtureActions unavailable flag. ***Consumer: apps/venue Dashboard/FixtureCard/FixtureActions.*** |
| `get_my_world()` | `getMyWorld()` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **READ/resolver (mig 372), SECDEF STABLE.** Everything for the signed-in person in one call. Returns `{ ok, person_id, player_fixtures: { league:[…], casual:[…] }, ref_assignments:[<game>…] (folds league+casual via get_my_assignments AND tournament via get_my_tournament_assignments, mig 443), club_memberships:[{ club_id, name, cohort_id, cohort_name, status }], guardian_of:[{ child_profile_id, first_name, last_name, sessions:[…] }], admin_roles:[{ type:'team_admin'|'venue_admin', entity_id, name, role }], coaching:[{ club_team_id, club_id, team_name, role }] (club_team_managers), conflicts:[{ kind:'play_vs_ref', play_game_id, play_context, play_kickoff, ref_game_id, ref_context, ref_kickoff, message }] }`. Conflict = playing one game while reffing another within a 2-hour window. **mig 373: `club_memberships` includes `status='paused'` (was active/ending only) so a frozen membership is SHOWN in the switcher (badged "Paused"), not hidden — access stays restricted (`member_book_class_session` blocks paused; `MemberPass.jsx` hides the QR for paused). `cancelled` still excluded.** Supersedes the `get_user_relationships` + `get_my_next_assignment` split for the phone hub. ***Consumer: apps/inorout multi-context hub (Phase 0c switcher).*** |
| `get_my_money()` | `getMyMoney()` | **authenticated** (anon REVOKED) | **READ/resolver (mig 404, Stripe Phase 2), SECDEF STABLE, read-only (no audit).** The signed-in human's whole money picture in one call — the "Dave" persona. Identity resolved exactly like `get_my_world` (auth.uid → people.id for casual, → member_profiles.id for memberships). Returns `{ ok, person_id, profile_id, memberships:[{ membership_id, who_for ('self'|child name), is_self, club_name, tier_name, period, amount_pence, status, renews_at, is_stripe }], charges:[{ charge_id, stream:'membership', who_for, is_self, label, amount_due_pence, paid_pence, status, due_date }], casual:[<get_my_payment_history row shape — folded in unchanged, whole-pounds `amount`>], summary:{ owed_pence, paid_count, upcoming_count } }`. **Memberships I'm responsible for = own (`member_profile_id`) ∪ as-payer (`payer_profile_id`, mig 403) ∪ as-guardian (`member_guardians`), deduped, non-cancelled.** Membership charges matched from `venue_charges` via `split_part(source_id,':',1)=membership_id` (source_type='membership'); `paid_pence` summed from non-voided `venue_payments`. **Casual fees (pence vs pounds) kept in a SEPARATE array — never summed across streams.** Casual logic in `get_my_payment_history` (mig 039) is UNCHANGED. NOTE: season one-off (mode=payment) Stripe payments not yet folded in (deferred to Phase 3, see DECISIONS). ***Consumer: apps/inorout MemberProfile "My money" section (Phase 2); future operator reporting (Phase 6).*** |

| `venue_seed_knockout(p_venue_token, p_tournament_event_id, p_competition_id)` | `venueSeedKnockout(venueToken, tournamentEventId, competitionId)` | anon + authenticated | **CHANGED mig 500 (Tournament Groups→KO PR#1) — now CONFIG-DRIVEN.** Reads `competitions.config.qualifiers_per_group` and takes the top-`qpg` of each group (`group_rank <= qpg`) instead of the hardcoded `IN (1,2)`. **BACKWARD COMPATIBLE:** absent key → `COALESCE(...,2)` → byte-identical top-2 bracket (the paid Epic-D venue-operator flow never sets it, so unchanged — reviewer-confirmed faithful reproduction of the mig-452 body + this one edit). ---

## ADDING A NEW RPC — CHECKLIST

1. Write SQL in Supabase SQL editor first — never via Claude Code
2. Use `SECURITY DEFINER`
3. `REVOKE ALL` from anon if authenticated-only
4. `GRANT EXECUTE` to correct role
5. Authenticate via `auth.uid()` or token param — never trust passed user_id
6. Return `jsonb`
7. Add wrapper in `packages/core/storage/supabase.js`
8. Export from `packages/core/index.js` barrel
9. Import at call site
10. Verify: grep confirms RPC name appears in exactly ONE `supabase.rpc()` call in supabase.js
